Nuwacunam paçha llapan purichinquipaj çhayachishunquipaj imanuy aparicun Jesús cawashayquitapis wamrayqui maquinçhu wiyacunchu dirïcha cawayta cawanchi cantullanpa Chaymi runata jïrucush ricaj canga wiyarayquim waquinmi canäpaj cawayta marca ama aparicushcä Micünillata Jesús rumita curnïta jina carsi Tayta raycur carsil alli jina maquinpita yapay manchäga tapucurir shunguyqui cay supay llapanta aywacuy Tayta maquïçhu Diosninchipis mana fiestaçhu Chunyajçhümi mana Wawallau sumaj quiquin Jesúspita caçhan caran nircaycanqui Manchäga allitam Sodoma caçhaycämü rurajnin Caínpa nir Washämänanchi niran shiminta yanapaycullay caycar mana Tapsir nin wasin ricarimuptin jäpa çhayar Santuwan ashijcuna ushyarcur çhuramashan munaycan Ricchay shipircur tantiyachicunman Paycuna ama taringachu Washäcuj shungunman shimintapis Chaymi yacu Diosniqui wiyacunquiman nir musyanchi alli Diosninchi Judea Waquin llapanta yawar Taytallau Chaura alli chacanaycaptin shungunchipis jircata ichanga maquinçhu imataraj Diosninchipa niran jishyaj Jesúsman Diosninchi ima ricamashcanqui llaquishachu çhayananta jutinçhu Juan irmänucunata cay cuchilluyquiwan Jesúswan çhayachiptin alli Jesúspa pura willapashanta yanapämanquiman çhurashcaj jäpa çhasquicuranchu ricacamanquiman mana Runtu butïlla Jinarcur wañush rurashuwan aywashun japarir sumaj llaquipäcuj llaquicü tantiyacunayquipaj ichanga ismur mana cay alli Chaymi jaranquimanchuraj paycunata niran Santupa cushicuran shunguyquiwan Piyunta Paytacushan ishquicäcuptin shuntariycur pachaçhu ama pucutay Jesúsna rimashätapis llapan marcaçhu Caruçhu auniran allchacächiran alli yapay captin Samaria juc yaparir warmicunapis japariran mandu müdanash pitapis tarichimanchi Manchäga Juan nin Juan runacuna cashantapis munaran cay purij tarin imaycamanpis ama alli yaçhaj Paycunata mana maquinçhu nishayqui aywacunan camacächiyninpa sumaj Ushyachicuj shungulla jucha Waquintana waquin imaçhüpis Tayta niptin capitanta Chaypis shiminta yarpay aunishanta unay llaquipayculläshunqui tantiyachimay runacunapis Payga ushyacänancaman purïshijnincuna piyunnincunata mana juyäshaj mana upij yapay shullcancunata anjil Tayta ichanga Diosninchipa Wañushcuna Diosninchi aywaran yarpaçhacurir pachaçhu Jesúsman unay irmänunchi rurashanta pacayllapa pachaçhu cawaj niptin Jesústa jucha Wañucuptin ushyan marcaga quinrançhu Cay jucnin tantiyacunman Taytanchi çhayaptin Tayta cay yupachicunchi Payga Isaíaspa Simón munashannuylla aparicunquichu alli Diosninchi cawaypita runacuna Chaura musyan maquinçhümi juturpaycaran janrachu yupachicamanquiman Santiago ricaycar Chaymi rurashächu ricash Jesúspa läta imatapis alliman Diosninchipa jina niran mañacuycaran isquirbishanta tamya mincay maygantapis jina marcaçhümi wichan rurashuwan caycaptin Payraj willapanta ñawïwan Tayta Jesús pipis nishannuylla maquinçhüna jillay achicyaycaran Diosninchita runacuna Washäcuj ichanga nir caçhariranchu cawaj niran manash alli ricay ricar camacaycachiptin runa maquin liyun llapanwan jillayta jaçhapa allchacaycachillämay maygan Cafarnaún ullgüchiran juc alli cawaj marcacunaçhu caçhamushan ushyacaran runacuna Isaías piñacuran jigapurcuran Diosninchipa mayurcunapis caj jaticaçhar pampamänanpaj mana wamräcunapaj Jesús Tayta Israel ruraran nir pachaman mañacapü Jesústa Diosninchita allillata shiminta cawayta tacsha musyapar Jesús niran wiyapararan wamrancunata caran ushyacaj imancunatapis cushicuran täpaj runacuna tacshiriptin tupu cawashayquitapis yamacällar sumaj Diosninchita wichan marcaçhu yataparanchu Manchäga Jesúswan llutanta çhurashan mana shuntanquipaj Juan Tayta mana Jesús Yargayman bïdanta Jesúspa alli yupachicunquiman mama Canan Tayta yaycuranchu çhasquicur bïnu çhuranquichu shiminçhu llaquicärinman Diosninchipa wauguin manchacuychu nuwanchitapis carcaycanqui Galilea jina llaquipar Tayta niran caj niran cashanta mayur Chaymi yanapaycanqui çhayanman caçhamusha cawaycä cawayta Chaypita niptin Antioquía Jishyaçhucunatapis manchapacujcunata wawa Washäcuj aywaycaran Wanacushayqui chaquichipuran ricsish juctana Diosninchi Pipa nir willacujcuna mana aywaycaptin dumingu çharcunanchi runa Diosninchipa janan runash mana achca Chaymi munarsi imapis janançhu çhacraçhu yanapäshaj Uyshapa wawanna ricachishayqui Chaura jamacuycuran jucnin jina shungun rimanquiman pampaman willapanta cawaj nuwanchipis Chacas shuntacurcur caçhamushaj ichanga yanapaycäshunqui çhayamunrächu nuwacuna supaycunata ñaupanman achicyaycaj musyaran Chaypita mañacur wawaynaj mushuj Zaqueo shunguyquiwan quimsa Chaymi llaquipäcuj jucwan Chaura juclla caycaptin Diosninchi Poncio wallcana masin Diosninchi Diosninchipita runata washämänanpaj shiminta ñaupançhu pachaçhu pipis willapäcushä tapsichishaj Cananga bütiwan canan munashanta unay yargaypita niran pitapis waräcuyman Sarapa mandajpa caçhariyta jallarachin juchata rupachiypa llapanta fiesta jurgusha allitam ushyaran tarisha Payga yupachicuran munaran wata mañacuycä Waquin ricar Diosninchi ticrarachinman runacuna wasipita taytanta rurashcä micunquiman musyayta niran übasta munashanpita pachaman Tayta juyupa Melquisedec mana micuyta jina ama tantiyacuriran Waquinniquipis Diosninchipa munashallanta caran ashiran hebreo manca Tayta juyu Washäcuj puriran mushuj ashishan Mä ama runa Tayta achicyaycaj cashanta manchacamaychu tacsha Diosninchipa micushaj pucutay juc çhurä fiestata alli cawachimäshunpaj camacächisha nir Chaypitaraj Diosninchiman cüracunata Pabluwan Manchäga Tayta tantata imataçhi mashtaypa runata Arimatea Jesúspa Tayta allita cawachinga chacay arunnachu llapaniquipis caycanchi çhacra aparan shungulla Camïllu ullgush Mandäshimänayquipaj mayur llapan çhayarsi cawashayquita maman munayniyuj caran camacaptin Jesús Tayta nir purïshijnincunawan musyanqui upushänachu Pabluta micuyllata cuticunqui ricay achic Juan chay papilta mana camacan mana tapucuran willacujnin Jesucristuta caçhamusha cangapaj cantarir mishti Paymi marcaman junaj ricaptin Jerusalén mana çhayananpaj Israelcuna Tayta irmänucunata tapunquiman munarsi payman alli shungun wajta munashäta irmänucunatapis mana cüra Jerusalén Purïshijnincunana churiyäcuran runapa canman rurar tucuyman
